  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            AKD.HideUnusedBlocks();
            ResizeCarouselParent();
            //If not in design mode start carousel, otherwise show contents.
            var designMode = "";
            try {
                designMode = document.forms[MSOWebPartPageFormName].MSOLayout_InDesignMode.value;
            } catch (e) {
                designMode = "0";
            }
            if (designMode != "1") {
                jQuery('.theme-carousel.owl-carousel').owlCarousel({
                    navigation: true,
                    slideSpeed: 300,
                    paginationSpeed: 400,
                    singleItem: true,
                    autoWidth: true,
                    responsive: true,
                    responsiveBaseElement: "#DeltaPlaceHolderMain",
                });
            }
            else {
                jQuery('.theme-carousel.owl-carousel').show();
            }
        });

        function ResizeCarouselParent() {
            var w = jQuery("#DeltaPlaceHolderMain").width();
            jQuery(".theme-carousel").parents("div").first().width(w);
        }

        //Dynamic resize for carousel
        jQuery(window).resize(function () {
            ResizeCarouselParent();
        });
  </script>

  <!-- Cookie consent -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   window.addEventListener("load", function(){
            window.cookieconsent.initialise({
                "palette": {
                    "popup": {
                        "background": "#edeff5",
                        "text": "#838391"
                    },
                    "button": {
                        "background": "#4b81e8"
                    }
                },
                "type": "opt-out",
                "content": {
                    "message": Resources.CookieLayerText, 
                    "dismiss": Resources.CookieLayerAcceptText,
                    "deny": Resources.CookieLayerDenyText, 
                    "link": Resources.CookieLayerMoreInfoLinkText, 
                    "href": Resources.CookieLayerMoreInfoLink 
                },
                "onInitialise": function (status) {
                    var type = this.options.type;
                    var didConsent = this.hasConsented();
                    if (type == 'opt-out' && !didConsent) {
                        //Disable cookies
                        disableGACookies();
                    }else{
                        //Enable cookies
                        enableGACookies();
                        //Add Google Analytics
                        addGA();
                        //Add Google Tag Manager
                        addGTM();
                    }
                },
                "onStatusChange": function(status) {
                    var type = this.options.type;
                    var didConsent = this.hasConsented();
                    if (type == 'opt-out' && !didConsent) {
                        //Disable cookies
                        disableGACookies();
                    }else{
                        //Enable cookies
                        enableGACookies();
                        //Add Google Analytics
                        addGA();
                        //Add Google Tag Manager
                        addGTM();
                    }
                },
                "onRevokeChoice": function() {
                    var type = this.options.type;
                    if (type == 'opt-out') {
                        //Enable cookies
                        enableGACookies();
                        //Add Google Analytics
                        addGA();
                        //Add Google Tag Manager
                        addGTM();
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        function disableGACookies(){

            // Disable tracking if the opt-out cookie exists.
            var disableStr = "";

            if(document.location.host == "acceptatie.akd.nl"){
                disableStr = 'ga-disable-' + 'UA-5397558-6';
            }else{
                disableStr = 'ga-disable-' + 'UA-5397558-1';
            }


            if (document.cookie.indexOf(disableStr + '=true') > -1) {
                window[disableStr] = true;
            }

            // Opt-out function
            document.cookie = disableStr + '=true; expires=Thu, 31 Dec 2099 23:59:59 UTC; path=/';
            window[disableStr] = true;

            //Delete other cookies
            var deleteCookies = "_ga";
            deleteCookie(deleteCookies, "/",".akd.nl");
            deleteCookies = "_gat";
            deleteCookie(deleteCookies, "/",".akd.nl");
            deleteCookies = "_gid";
            deleteCookie(deleteCookies, "/",".akd.nl");
        }

        function enableGACookies(){

            // Enable tracking.
            var disableStr = "";

            if(document.location.host == "acceptatie.akd.nl"){
                disableStr = 'ga-disable-' + 'UA-5397558-6';
            }else{
                disableStr = 'ga-disable-' + 'UA-5397558-1';
            }
            deleteCookie(disableStr, "/", document.location.host);
        }
        
        function getCookie(name) {
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
        }
        
        function deleteCookie(name, path, domain) {
            //Cookies cant be deleted, you need to set an expires date in the past.
            //console.log("------- DELETE COOKIE -------");
            //console.log("name: " + name);
            //console.log("path: " + path);
            //console.log("domain: " + domain);
            var valueCookie = getCookie(name);
            //console.log("value: " + valueCookie);
            if(valueCookie != undefined){
                var cookie = name + '=' + valueCookie + '; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; path=' + path +'; domain='+ domain;
                //console.log("cookie: " + cookie);
                document.cookie = cookie;
            }else{
                //console.log("cookie: NO COOKIE");
            }
        }

        function addGA(){
            if(!document.cookie.indexOf("ga-disable-") >=0){
                (function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){
                    (i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)},i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
                    m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
                })(window,document,'script','https://www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');
                if(document.location.host == "acceptatie.akd.nl"){
                    ga('create', 'UA-5397558-6', 'auto');
                }else{
                    ga('create', 'UA-5397558-1', 'auto');
                }
                ga('set', 'forceSSL', true); // Toelichting CBP: Gebruik altijd https voor Google Analytics
                ga('set', 'anonymizeIp', true); // Toelichting CBP: Zet de IP-maskering aan
                ga('send', 'pageview');
            }
        }

        function addGTM(){
            if(!document.cookie.indexOf("ga-disable-") >=0){
                (function(w,d,s,l,i){w[l]=w[l]||[];w[l].push({'gtm.start':
                new Date().getTime(),event:'gtm.js'});var f=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0],
                j=d.createElement(s),dl=l!='dataLayer'?'&l='+l:'';j.async=true;j.src=
                'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id='+i+dl;f.parentNode.insertBefore(j,f);
                })(window,document,'script','dataLayer','GTM-W3FCNF2');
            }
        }
  </script>

                <span>
                 Persoonlijke relatie
                </span>
                <span id="WebPartCaptionWPQ1">
                </span>
               </h2>
              </span>
             </div>
             <div allowdelete="false" class="ms-WPBody ms-wpContentDivSpace " haspers="false" id="WebPartWPQ1" style="" webpartid="96f68e6b-fcee-4c05-bc28-3e08919be1b8" width="100%">
              <div class="ms-rtestate-field">
               <p>
                <span class="ms-rteFontSize-2">
                 Bij AKD hechten we veel belang aan een goede, persoonlijke relatie. U heeft altijd een aanspreekpunt die thuis is in uw vraagstukken, branche en organisatie. Daarbij kunt u rekenen op snelle - to the point - reacties, ook op partnerniveau.

              <div class="ms-rtestate-field">
               <p>
                AKD is actief in een groot aantal rechtsgebieden. Door de combinatie van verregaande specialisatie, ruime ervaring en nauw samenwerken ontvangt u het beste advies voor al uw juridische en fiscale vraagstukken. Precies zoals u dat mag verwachten van een adviseur.
